Hello London,

Thank you very much all your hard work and public-spiritedness for
Tuesday's Open House.

I am attaching some photos for the day and there is=A0an entry in
Maestro (Marcom London Projects > Clerkenwell Design Week) that you
can allocate your time against.

There were a lot of eager students (with time on their hands between
4-6pm), but the IDEO logo also appeared slap bang in the middle of
maps issued to anyone who engaged with the festival - 24,000 people
registered to attend in 2011.

Particular thanks to:
Ben for his vision and then making that concrete, quickly
Lydia for her Whose Life insights
Amy for Brainstorming
Kristjana and Haiyan for bringing OpenIDEO to life
Bobbie, Jamie and Lorraine for making it an awesome experience
Steve and AK for engaging people in conversation
and allll the rest of the team.

Nadine

--047d7b2e0d8defc59104c0c6a878
